description
"[size=18][b]This is for [b][url=http://www.indycon.org]IndyCon 2020 [/url][/b]attendees only.[/b][/size][i] Translation = If you do not have an IndyCon ticket [b]do not list items, do not bid,[/b] and [b]do not contact the seller[/b].[/i]\n\nIf you are attending IndyCon (meaning you have already purchased a ticket), use [b]this Geeklist[/b] to sell, buy, trade, auction, or give away your games. It is up to you. Make sure the terms and description of the game are clear and accurate. Once an item is sold (or traded) edit the item listing to \"Sold\" ([b]don't delete it[/b] - that makes the list confusing). \n\nAt IndyCon there will be a shelf for games that have been sold. If you use the shelf make sure the game is marked as sold, the amount agreed upon, with buyer's name, and your (the seller's) name and cell phone number. On Friday, only sold games will be allowed on the shelf. Saturday at noon, the shelf should be opened up for games that have not sold yet as well. \n\nIf you do strike a deal here on BGG, you are on your own honor to pay them the 3%.\n\n[b]Have fun and play nice.[/b] Last year the list reached over 1,500 games with some of the best deals that I have ever seen.\n\nGeekmail me with questions or use the comments section. You can also use the comments section to request a certain game that you would like to see listed (do not create a listing for it here).\n\n[u]Because this Geeklist will get large, here are two ways you can help keep track of your stuff on it:[/u]\n[i]One easy way to track [b]your listings[/b] down is to go to [b]My Geek - Profile - Contributions[/b] and then click on the number next to [b]\"Geeklist Items\"[/b] on the right side of the screen. It will bring up the items you listed (from newest to oldest) along with links.\n\nYou can do the same with [b]your bids[/b] by going to [b]My Geek - Profile - Contributions [/b]and then the number next to [b]\"Geeklist Item Comments\"[/b].[/i]\n\nIf you have questions please geekmail me."
